# Symbolic Regression with Genetic Programming


Date: Jun 14 2026 // 13:55:59


C++ Version: Apple clang version 21.0.0 (clang-2100.1.1.101)
Target: arm64-apple-darwin25.5.0
Thread model: posix

<span style='color:blue;'>Experiment: ex_4_refactored

</span>

Author: James McArdle


This program performs symbolic regression using a simple genetic programming approach.


It reads input data from a binary file, generates mathematical expressions, evaluates them against the data, and evolves the expressions over multiple generations to find better fits.

- Output file:       (null)
- Tolerance:         0.01
- Cutoff Score:      100
- Max Floats:        1024
- Max Floats:        1024
